            <div style="margin-bottom:12px;height:50px;"><a href="/gp/redirect.html/ref=amb_link_85606691_1?location=http://www.omnivoracious.com/&token=7B08D69EFB23F01C31332A4EB1A38F4804AAB087&pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-blog-0&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=493985451&pf_rd_i=283155"><img src="http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/daily/lozenge/lozenge_omni._V230191888_.jpg" align="left" alt="Amazon Omnivoracious" border="0" /></a></div><div class="unified_widget rcmBody"><h2>2010 Edgar Award Winners</h2><a href="/Last-Child-John-Hart/dp/0312642369/ref=amb_link_353013782_1?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-1&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=1261969522&pf_rd_i=283155"><img src="http://ecx.images-amazon.com/images/P/0312642369.01._SL110_PIsitb-sticker-arrow-sm,TopRight,10,-13_PE32_OU01_SCLZZZZZZZ_V207185439_.jpg" width="88" align="left" alt="The Last Child" height="133" border="0" /></a> 
Discover the winners of the 2010 <a href="/gp/feature.html/ref=amb_link_353013782_2?ie=UTF8&docId=151303&pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-1&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=1261969522&pf_rd_i=283155">Edgar Awards</a>, sponsored by the Mystery Writers of America: <a href="/gp/entity/store/B001H6PTG6/ref=amb_link_353013782_3?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-1&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=1261969522&pf_rd_i=283155">John Hart</a>'s <a href="/Last-Child-John-Hart/dp/0312642369/ref=amb_link_353013782_4?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-1&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=1261969522&pf_rd_i=283155"><i>The Last Child</i></a> takes the award for Best Novel, and <a href="/gp/entity/store/B001SQ8I0Y/ref=amb_link_353013782_5?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-1&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=1261969522&pf_rd_i=283155">Stefanie Pintoff</a>'s acclaimed debut, <a href="/Shadow-Gotham-Stefanie-Pintoff/dp/0312628129/ref=amb_link_353013782_6?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-1&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=1261969522&pf_rd_i=283155"><i>In the Shadow of Gotham</i></a>, is awarded Best First Novel.<br clear="left"><p class="seeMore"><span class="carat">&#8250;</span><a href="/Awards-Books/b/ref=amb_link_353013782_7?ie=UTF8&node=542942&pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=right-1&pf_rd_r=1RVCMGP6WPZF34Z5GVPD&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=1261969522&pf_rd_i=283155">See more Award Winners in Books</a></p><div class="h_rule"></div></div><div class="unified_widget rcm widget">

<script type="text/javascript"> 
var ZeitgeistFVP = {
    popover: null,
    popoverText: "Amazon Bestsellers lists are updated hourly. Between list updates, the price of an item may change from being free to having a price and vice versa. Although the item's price changes immediately, the list and its rankings stay the same until the next hourly update.",
    displayPaidList: function(widgetID) {
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidTab_" + widgetID).addClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeTab_" + widgetID).removeClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidList_" + widgetID).show();
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeList_" + widgetID).hide();
    },
    displayFreeList: function(widgetID) {
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeTab_" + widgetID).addClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidTab_" + widgetID).removeClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidList_" + widgetID).hide();
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeList_" + widgetID).show();
    },
    displayPricePopover: function(anchor, title) {
        if (ZeitgeistFVP.popover) {
            ZeitgeistFVP.popover.close();
        }
        ZeitgeistFVP.popover = jQuery.AmazonPopover.displayPopover({
            literalContent: ZeitgeistFVP.popoverText,
            location: "bottom",
            locationAlign: "center",
            locationElement: anchor,
            modal: false,
            showCloseButton: true,
            title: title,
            closeText: "close",
            width: 316
        });
    }
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript"> 
var ZeitgeistFVP = {
    popover: null,
    popoverText: "Amazon Bestsellers lists are updated hourly. Between list updates, the price of an item may change from being free to having a price and vice versa. Although the item's price changes immediately, the list and its rankings stay the same until the next hourly update.",
    displayPaidList: function(widgetID) {
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidTab_" + widgetID).addClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeTab_" + widgetID).removeClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidList_" + widgetID).show();
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeList_" + widgetID).hide();
    },
    displayFreeList: function(widgetID) {
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeTab_" + widgetID).addClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidTab_" + widgetID).removeClass("zg_explore_currentTab");
        jQuery("#zgTopPaidList_" + widgetID).hide();
        jQuery("#zgTopFreeList_" + widgetID).show();
    },
    displayPricePopover: function(anchor, title) {
        if (ZeitgeistFVP.popover) {
            ZeitgeistFVP.popover.close();
        }
        ZeitgeistFVP.popover = jQuery.AmazonPopover.displayPopover({
            literalContent: ZeitgeistFVP.popoverText,
            location: "bottom",
            locationAlign: "center",
            locationElement: anchor,
            modal: false,
            showCloseButton: true,
            title: title,
            closeText: "close",
            width: 316
        });
    }
}

<script type="text/JavaScript"> 
amznJQ.onReady('JQuery', function() { (function($) {
    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = false;
    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = false;
    $("#rhf_container").show();
    var rhfShvlEventHandler = function () {
        if (   ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded
            && ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading
            && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0 ) {
            var yPosition = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
            var rhfElementFound = $('#rhfMainHeading').size();
            var rhfPosition = $('#rhfMainHeading').offset().top;
            if (/webkit.*mobile/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                rhfPosition -= $(window).scrollTop();
            }
            if (rhfElementFound && ( rhfPosition - yPosition < 400 )) {
                window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = true;
                $.ajax({
                    url: '/gp/history/external/full-rhf-rec-handler.html',
                    type: "POST",
                    timeout: 30000,
                    data: { shovelerName   : 'rhf',
                      key            : 'rhf',
                      numToPreload   : '5',
                      isGateway      : 0,
                      refTag         : 'pd_rhf_shvl',
                      parentSession  : '182-0202755-3246608',
                      excludeASIN    : '',
                      renderPopover  : 0,
                      forceSprites   : 0 },
                    success: function(responseText, textStatus, XMLHttpRequest) {
                        $("#rhf_container").html(responseText);
                        $("#rhfShvl").trigger("render-shoveler");
                        window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = true;
                    },
                    error: function(responseText, textStatus, XMLHttpRequest) {
                        $("#rhf_container").hide();
                        $("#rhf_error").show();
                        return;
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    }
    $(document).ready(rhfShvlEventHandler);
    $(window).scroll(rhfShvlEventHandler);
})(jQuery); });
</script>
